;editorialChanges{The digitization seems to be based on two different publications. First part seems to be based on some other edition, maybe Abhidhanasangraha, Nirnayasagara edition. The second part seems to be based on the edition mentioned above. It is not clearly demarcated where this change occurs. The numberings are also not consistent with Nirnayasagara press edition. Therefore the page numbers have not been mentioned in the digitization. There is a misnumbering in trisvarakanda in printed edition which has led to some verse number anomalies. Verse number 208 is missing, and there are two verses having numbering of 235 in trisvarakanda. In digitization, the verse 208 is shown missing. But after verse 235, the numbers are carried till 410 and then there are two verses 410 to come up to the printed edition numbers from verse 410 onwards.}
